## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the rate of change of concentration (dA/dt) as a function of time and concentration A, which is a classic chemical kinetics problem. The rate law typically depends on the concentration raised to some power (reaction order), and may involve more complex mechanisms like autocatalysis or reversible reactions.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Zero-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0', 'scenario': 'Constant rate of consumption/production independent of concentration'}
- {'name': 'First-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A', 'scenario': 'Rate proportional to concentration (radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition)'}
- {'name': 'Second-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Bimolecular reaction where rate depends on square of concentration'}
- {'name': 'nth-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1', 'scenario': 'General power-law kinetics with fractional or arbitrary reaction order'}
- {'name': 'Reversible first-order reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1', 'scenario': 'First-order forward reaction with reverse reaction approaching equilibrium'}
- {'name': 'Mixed-order / parallel reactions', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Simultaneous first- and second-order pathways'}
- {'name': 'Autocatalytic reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A)', 'scenario': 'Product catalyzes its own formation, logistic-type kinetics'}
- {'name': 'Saturation kinetics (substrate inhibition)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2)', 'scenario': 'Enzyme kinetics with substrate inhibition at high concentrations'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent rate coefficient (power-law)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * t**c1 * A', 'scenario': 'Diffusion-limited or fractal kinetics where rate constant changes with time'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent exponential deactivation', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A', 'scenario': 'Catalyst deactivation or time-varying rate constant'}
- {'name': 'Consecutive/complex mechanism', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**c2 + c3', 'scenario': 'Multi-step reaction mechanism with different order contributions'}
- {'name': 'Rational rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A)', 'scenario': 'Enzyme-like or surface-catalyzed reaction with saturation'}
- {'name': 'Sigmoidal cooperative kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (A**c1 + c2)', 'scenario': 'Cooperative binding or allosteric enzyme kinetics'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative rate with increasing concentration → decay kinetics, dA_dt = -k * A^n with k > 0
- Rate approaching zero at large A → saturation kinetics, rational function A/(1+A) structure
- Rate changing sign at specific concentration → reversible reaction with equilibrium, linear form c0*A + c1
- Rate maximum at intermediate concentration → autocatalytic or substrate-inhibition mechanism, quadratic in denominator or A*(K-A) form
- Rate constant effectively varying with time → diffusion-controlled kinetics, multiply rate by t^c or exp(c*t)
- Concave-up log(|dA_dt|) vs log(A) plot → power-law kinetics with order > 1
- Linear log(|dA_dt|) vs log(A) → simple nth-order kinetics, use A**c form
- Rate independent of A but dependent on t → zero-order in A with time-dependent source/sink
